   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    9/11 Truth movement
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
     <span class="mw-redirectedfrom">
      (Redirected from
      <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_Movement&amp;redirect=no" title="9/11 Truth Movement">
       9/11 Truth Movement
      </a>
      )
     </span>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
     Jump to:
     <a href="#mw-head">
      navigation
     </a>
     ,
     <a href="#p-search">
      search
     </a>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:9-11_Truth_1.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1174" data-file-width="2048" height="172" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/9-11_Truth_1.jpg/300px-9-11_Truth_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/9-11_Truth_1.jpg/450px-9-11_Truth_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/9-11_Truth_1.jpg/600px-9-11_Truth_1.jpg 2x" width="300"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:9-11_Truth_1.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Supporters of the 9/11 Truth movement at an anti-war demonstration in Los Angeles, October 2007
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Adherents of the
      <b>
       9/11 Truth movement
      </b>
      are
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Conspiracy_theorists" title="Conspiracy theorists">
       conspiracy theorists
      </a>
      who dispute the mainstream account of the
      <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">
       September 11 attacks
      </a>
      of 2001. The "truthers", as they are, sometimes
      <a href="/wiki/Pejorative_suffix" title="Pejorative suffix">
       pejoratively
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT22LS_1-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-NYT22LS-1">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        1
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PSM19CNC_2-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-PSM19CNC-2">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        2
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      called, dispute the commonly accepted account that
      <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda" title="Al-Qaeda">
       Al-Qaeda
      </a>
      terrorists hijacked four airliners, crashed them into
      <a href="/wiki/The_Pentagon" title="The Pentagon">
       the Pentagon
      </a>
      and New York's
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Twin_Towers_(NYC)" title="Twin Towers (NYC)">
       Twin Towers
      </a>
      , whereupon the crashes led to
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_collapse_of_the_Twin_Towers" title="The collapse of the Twin Towers">
       the collapse of the Twin Towers
      </a>
      . "Truthers" primarily focus on what they claim are significant inconsistencies in that explanation, suggesting a
      <a href="/wiki/Censorship" title="Censorship">
       cover-up
      </a>
      and, at the least, complicity by
      <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks_advance-knowledge_conspiracy_theories" title="September 11 attacks advance-knowledge conspiracy theories">
       insiders
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Feuer_3-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Feuer-3">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        3
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rudin_4-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Rudin-4">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        4
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Barber_5-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Barber-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Powell_6-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Powell-6">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        6
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Barry_7-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Barry-7">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        7
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hunt_8-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Hunt-8">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        8
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kay_9-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Kay-9">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        9
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">
       <a href="#cite_note-10">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        10
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      They analyze evidence from the attacks, discuss different
      <a href="/wiki/9/11_conspiracy_theories" title="9/11 conspiracy theories">
       theories
      </a>
      about how the attacks happened and call for a new investigation into the attacks.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morales_11-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Morales-11">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        11
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Olivier_12-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Olivier-12">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        12
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">
       <a href="#cite_note-13">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        13
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">
       <a href="#cite_note-14">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        14
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">
       <a href="#cite_note-15">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        15
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-eastvalleytribune_16-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-eastvalleytribune-16">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        16
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Stratford_Gazette_17-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Stratford_Gazette-17">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        17
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Some of the organizations assert that there is evidence that individuals within the
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_government" title="United States government">
       United States government
      </a>
      may have been either responsible for or knowingly complicit in the September 11 attacks. Motives suggested by the movement include the use of the attacks as a pretext to start wars in
      <a href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001present)">
       Afghanistan
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Iraq_War" title="Iraq War">
       Iraq
      </a>
      and to create opportunities to curtail
      <a href="/wiki/Civil_liberties" title="Civil liberties">
       civil liberties
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rudin_4-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Rudin-4">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        4
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Manjoo_18-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Manjoo-18">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        18
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Support for the movement is negligible from professionals in relevant fields, such as civil and aerospace engineering.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">
       <a href="#cite_note-19">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        19
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
     </p>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Characteristics">
       Characteristics
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Characteristics">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Name">
       Name
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Name">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:911InsideJobSticker.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="768" data-file-width="1024" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/911InsideJobSticker.jpg/220px-911InsideJobSticker.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/911InsideJobSticker.jpg/330px-911InsideJobSticker.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/911InsideJobSticker.jpg/440px-911InsideJobSticker.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:911InsideJobSticker.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Truth movement sticker
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      "9/11 Truth movement" is the collective name of loosely affiliated
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Manjoo_18-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Manjoo-18">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        18
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bunch_20-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Bunch-20">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        20
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      organizations and individuals that question whether the United States government, agencies of the United States or individuals within such agencies were either responsible for or purposefully complicit in the
      <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">
       September 11 attacks
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Barber_5-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Barber-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Powell_6-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Powell-6">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        6
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Barry_7-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Barry-7">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        7
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hunt_8-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Hunt-8">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        8
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kay_9-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Kay-9">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        9
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kennedy_21-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Kennedy-21">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        21
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mol.C3.A9_22-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Mol.C3.A9-22">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        22
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sales_23-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Sales-23">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        23
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The term is also being used by the adherents of the movement,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Grossman_24-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Grossman-24">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        24
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harvey_25-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Harvey-25">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        25
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      who call themselves "9/11 skeptics",
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CBC-Speculation_26-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-CBC-Speculation-26">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        26
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      "truth activists",
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Curiel_27-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Curiel-27">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        27
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      or "9/11 Truthers",
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gravois_28-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Gravois-28">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        28
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      while generally rejecting the term "conspiracy theorists".
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bunch_20-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Bunch-20">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        20
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Curiel_27-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Curiel-27">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        27
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Adherents">
       Adherents
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Adherents">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      Adherents of the 9/11 Truth movement come from diverse social backgrounds.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Feuer_3-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Feuer-3">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        3
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harvey_25-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Harvey-25">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        25
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Curiel_27-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-Curiel-27">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        27
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The movement draws adherents from people of diverse political beliefs including
      <a href="/wiki/Modern_liberalism_in_the_United_States" title="Modern liberalism in the United States">
       liberals
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Conservatism_in_the_United_States" title="Conservatism in the United States">
       conservatives
      </a>
      , and
      <a href="/wiki/Libertarianism_in_the_United_States" title="Libertarianism in the United States">
       libertarians
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Barber_5-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-Barber-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mol.C3.A9_22-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Mol.C3.A9-22">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        22
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Curiel_27-3">
       <a href="#cite_note-Curiel-27">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        27
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Lev Grossman of
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Time_(magazine)" title="Time (magazine)">
        Time
       </a>
      </i>
      magazine has stated that support for the 9/11 Truth movement is not a "fringe phenomenon", but "a mainstream political reality."
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Grossman_24-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Grossman-24">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        24
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      However, others, such as Ben Smith of
      <i>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Politico_(newspaper)" title="Politico (newspaper)">
        Politico
       </a>
      </i>
      and the
      <i>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Minneapolis_Star_Tribune" title="Minneapolis Star Tribune">
        Minneapolis Star Tribune
       </a>
      </i>
      have stated that the movement has been "relegated to the fringe".
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">
       <a href="#cite_note-29">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        29
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">
       <a href="#cite_note-30">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        30
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/The_Washington_Post" title="The Washington Post">
        The Washington Post
       </a>
      </i>
      editorial staff went further describing the movement as "lunatic fringe."
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">
       <a href="#cite_note-31">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        31
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Mark Fenster, a
      <a href="/wiki/University_of_Florida" title="University of Florida">
       University of Florida
      </a>
      law professor and author of the book
      <i>
       Conspiracy Theories: Secrecy and Power in American Culture
      </i>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">
       <a href="#cite_note-32">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        32
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      says that "the amount of organisation" of the movement is significantly stronger than the organization of the movement related to doubts about the official account of the assassination of former United States President
      <a href="/wiki/John_F._Kennedy" title="John F. Kennedy">
       John F. Kennedy
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Barber_5-3">
       <a href="#cite_note-Barber-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      though this is likely the result of
      <a href="/wiki/New_media" title="New media">
       new media
      </a>
      technologies, such as online social networks, blogs, etc.
     </p>
     <p>
      The 9/11 Truth movement is active in the United States as well as in other countries.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Stratford_Gazette_17-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Stratford_Gazette-17">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        17
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In 2004,
      <a href="/wiki/John_Buchanan_(American_politician)" title="John Buchanan (American politician)">
       John Buchanan
      </a>
      ran for president on a 9/11 Truth platform.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">
       <a href="#cite_note-33">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        33
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">
       <a href="#cite_note-34">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        34
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <a href="/wiki/Jeff_Boss" title="Jeff Boss">
       Jeff Boss
      </a>
      ran in the 2012 US presidential election on a 9/11 Truth platform.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">
       <a href="#cite_note-35">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        35
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In a 2011 article in
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Skeptical_Inquirer" title="Skeptical Inquirer">
        Skeptical Inquirer
       </a>
      </i>
      , Bartlett and Miller do an overview and analyze the members of the 9/11 Truth movement community. The authors find that people involved in this movement, which seemingly is a disparate group with very diversified backgrounds, could be classified into three groups. They join the movement for different reasons, loosely self-assemble to fill different roles and are united by their shared mistrust in experts and the establishment (government and reputable sources of knowledge), and conspiratorial stance. Through their engagement, they each find their own fulfillment and satisfaction. Together, they contribute to the persistence, resilience and exaggerated claims of acceptance (in general public) of the movement.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bartlett_36-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Bartlett-36">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        36
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Views">
       Views
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Views">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">
      Main article:
      <a href="/wiki/9/11_conspiracy_theories" title="9/11 conspiracy theories">
       9/11 conspiracy theories
      </a>
     </div>
     <p>
      Many adherents of the 9/11 Truth movement suspect that United States government insiders played a part in the attacks, or may have known the attacks were imminent, and did nothing to alert others or stop them.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CBC-Speculation_26-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-CBC-Speculation-26">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        26
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Some within the movement who argue that insiders within the United States government were directly responsible for the September 11 attacks often allege that the attacks were planned and executed in order to provide the U.S. with a pretext for going to war in the Middle East, and, by extension, as a means of consolidating and extending the power of the Bush Administration.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Grossman_24-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-Grossman-24">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        24
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harvey_25-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-Harvey-25">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        25
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      According to these allegations, this would have given the Bush administration the justification for more widespread abuses of civil liberties and to invade Afghanistan and Iraq to ensure future supplies of oil.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CBC-Speculation_26-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-CBC-Speculation-26">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        26
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      In some cases, even in the mainstream media, "hawks" in the
      <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">
       White House
      </a>
      , especially former Vice President
      <a href="/wiki/Dick_Cheney" title="Dick Cheney">
       Dick Cheney
      </a>
      , and members of the
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Project_for_the_New_American_Century" title="Project for the New American Century">
        Project for the New American Century
       </a>
      </i>
      , a neoconservative think tank, have been accused of involvement in or awareness of the alleged plot.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sullivan_37-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Sullivan-37">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        37
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jacobson_38-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Jacobson-38">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        38
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Manjoo-Anthrax_39-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Manjoo-Anthrax-39">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        39
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Many adherents of the 9/11 Truth movement allege that the buildings of the World Trade Center were destroyed by
      <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Center_controlled_demolition_conspiracy_theories" title="World Trade Center controlled demolition conspiracy theories">
       controlled demolition
      </a>
      , a theory of major importance for the 9/11 Truth movement.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Feuer_3-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-Feuer-3">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        3
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mol.C3.A9_22-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-Mol.C3.A9-22">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        22
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tobin_40-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Tobin-40">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        40
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Communication">
       Communication
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Communication">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      The Internet plays a large role both in the communication between adherents and between local groups of the 9/11 Truth movement and in the dissemination of the views of the movement to the public at large.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rudin_4-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-Rudin-4">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        4
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Barber_5-4">
       <a href="#cite_note-Barber-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hunt_8-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-Hunt-8">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        8
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Grossman_24-3">
       <a href="#cite_note-Grossman-24">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        24
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jacobson_38-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Jacobson-38">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        38
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Colorado_Public_Television" title="Colorado Public Television">
       Colorado Public Television
      </a>
      has aired several films produced by the movement such as
      <i>
       9/11 Explosive Evidence: Experts Speak Out
      </i>
      , a documentary produced by
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Architects_and_Engineers_for_9/11_Truth" title="Architects and Engineers for 9/11 Truth">
       Architects and Engineers for 9/11 Truth
      </a>
      , which once was one of the "most shared" and "most watched" programs on the national
      <a href="/wiki/PBS" title="PBS">
       PBS
      </a>
      site. The station's airing of such films has been controversial for the affiliate and PBS.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">
       <a href="#cite_note-41">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        41
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">
       <a href="#cite_note-42">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        42
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="History">
       History
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: History">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      In the aftermath of the September 11 attacks, different interpretations of the events that questioned the account given by the U.S. government were published. Among others,
      <a href="/wiki/Michael_Ruppert" title="Michael Ruppert">
       Michael Ruppert
      </a>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">
       <a href="#cite_note-43">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        43
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and Canadian journalist
      <a href="/wiki/Barrie_Zwicker" title="Barrie Zwicker">
       Barrie Zwicker
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">
       <a href="#cite_note-44">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        44
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      published criticisms or pointed out purported anomalies of the accepted account of the attacks. French author
      <a href="/wiki/Jean-Charles_Brisard" title="Jean-Charles Brisard">
       Jean-Charles Brisard
      </a>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45">
       <a href="#cite_note-45">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        45
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and German authors
      <a href="/wiki/Mathias_Br%C3%B6ckers" title="Mathias Brckers">
       Mathias Brckers
      </a>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">
       <a href="#cite_note-46">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        46
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Andreas_von_B%C3%BClow" title="Andreas von Blow">
       Andreas von Blow
      </a>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">
       <a href="#cite_note-47">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        47
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      published books critical of media reporting and advancing the controlled demolition thesis of the destruction of the World Trade Center towers. In September 2002, the first "Bush Did It!" rallies and marches were held in
      <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco" title="San Francisco">
       San Francisco
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Oakland,_California" title="Oakland, California">
       Oakland, California
      </a>
      organized by The All People's Coalition.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">
       <a href="#cite_note-48">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        48
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <div class="thumb tleft">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:911TruthProtestSign.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2736" data-file-width="3648" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/911TruthProtestSign.jpg/220px-911TruthProtestSign.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/911TruthProtestSign.jpg/330px-911TruthProtestSign.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/911TruthProtestSign.jpg/440px-911TruthProtestSign.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:911TruthProtestSign.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        A 9/11 Truth movement protest sign, October 2009
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      In October 2004, the organization
      <i>
       9/11 Truth
      </i>
      released a statement, signed by nearly 200 people, including many relatives of people who perished on September 11, 2001, that calls for an investigation into the attacks. It also asserted that unanswered questions would suggest that people within the administration of President George W. Bush may have deliberately allowed the attacks to happen. Actor
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Edward_Asner" title="Edward Asner">
       Edward Asner
      </a>
      , former presidential candidate
      <a href="/wiki/Ralph_Nader" title="Ralph Nader">
       Ralph Nader
      </a>
      , former congresswoman
      <a href="/wiki/Cynthia_McKinney" title="Cynthia McKinney">
       Cynthia McKinney
      </a>
      , former assistant secretary of housing
      <a href="/wiki/Catherine_Austin_Fitts" title="Catherine Austin Fitts">
       Catherine Austin Fitts
      </a>
      , author
      <a href="/wiki/Richard_Heinberg" title="Richard Heinberg">
       Richard Heinberg
      </a>
      ,
      <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Enver_Masud&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Enver Masud (page does not exist)">
       Enver Masud
      </a>
      , founder of The Wisdom Fund, professors
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Richard_Falk" title="Richard Falk">
       Richard Falk
      </a>
      of the University of California,
      <a href="/wiki/Mark_Crispin_Miller" title="Mark Crispin Miller">
       Mark Crispin Miller
      </a>
      of New York University, Douglas Sturm of Bucknell University, Burns H. Weston of the University of Iowa College of Law and others signed the statement. In 2009,
      <a href="/wiki/Van_Jones" title="Van Jones">
       Van Jones
      </a>
      , a former advisor to President Obama, said he hadn't fully reviewed the statement before he signed and that the petition did not reflect his views "now or ever."
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-salon-petition_49-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-salon-petition-49">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        49
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">
       <a href="#cite_note-50">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        50
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">
       <a href="#cite_note-51">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        51
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In 2006,
      <a href="/wiki/Steven_E._Jones" title="Steven E. Jones">
       Steven E. Jones
      </a>
      , who became a leading academic voice of the demolition theory,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rudin_4-3">
       <a href="#cite_note-Rudin-4">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        4
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      published the paper "Why Indeed Did the WTC Buildings Completely Collapse?".
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYTCountersTheories_52-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-NYTCountersTheories-52">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        52
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He was placed on paid leave by
      <a href="/wiki/Brigham_Young_University" title="Brigham Young University">
       Brigham Young University
      </a>
      following what they described as Jones's "increasingly speculative and accusatory" statements in September 2006, pending a review of his statements and research. Six weeks later, Jones retired from the university.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jones_53-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Jones-53">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        53
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In the same year, 61 legislators in the U.S. State of Wisconsin signed a petition calling for the dismissal of a
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/University_of_Wisconsin" title="University of Wisconsin">
       University of Wisconsin
      </a>
      lecturer
      <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_Barrett_(Islamologist)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Kevin Barrett (Islamologist) (page does not exist)">
       Kevin Barrett
      </a>
      , after he joined the group
      <i>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Scholars_for_9/11_Truth" title="Scholars for 9/11 Truth">
        Scholars for 9/11 Truth
       </a>
      </i>
      . Citing
      <a href="/wiki/Academic_freedom" title="Academic freedom">
       academic freedom
      </a>
      , the university
      <a href="/wiki/Provost_(education)" title="Provost (education)">
       provost
      </a>
      declined to take action against Barrett.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54">
       <a href="#cite_note-54">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        54
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">
       <a href="#cite_note-55">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        55
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Guardian-Asquith-2006_56-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Guardian-Asquith-2006-56">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        56
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Several organizations of family members of people who have died in the attacks are calling for an independent investigation into the attacks.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57">
       <a href="#cite_note-57">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        57
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      In 2009, a group of people, including 9/11 Truth movement activist
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lorie_Van_Auken" title="Lorie Van Auken">
       Lorie Van Auken
      </a>
      and others who have lost friends or relatives in the attack, appealed to the City of New York to investigate the disaster.
      <i>
       The New York City Coalition for Accountability Now
      </i>
      collected signatures to require the
      <a href="/wiki/New_York_City_Council" title="New York City Council">
       New York City Council
      </a>
      to place the creation of an investigating commission on the November 2009 election ballot.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58">
       <a href="#cite_note-58">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        58
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The group collected more than enough signatures to put the proposal before the voters, but New York Supreme Court Justice Edward Lehner stated that the petition overstepped what is allowable by city law, and ruled that, despite wording in the petition to allow for elements ruled invalid to be stricken, it would not be allowed to appear on the ballot.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59">
       <a href="#cite_note-59">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        59
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60">
       <a href="#cite_note-60">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        60
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="9.2F11_Commission_Report_reaction">
       9/11 Commission Report reaction
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 9/11 Commission Report reaction">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      To the consternation of the families and adherents of the 9/11 Truth movement, many of the questions that the
      <a href="/wiki/9/11_Family_Steering_Committee" title="9/11 Family Steering Committee">
       9/11 Family Steering Committee
      </a>
      put to the
      <a href="/wiki/9/11_Commission" title="9/11 Commission">
       9/11 Commission
      </a>
      , chaired by former
      <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">
       New Jersey
      </a>
      Governor
      <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Kean" title="Thomas Kean">
       Thomas Kean
      </a>
      , were not asked in either the hearings nor in the Commission Report.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61">
       <a href="#cite_note-61">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        61
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lorie_Van_Auken" title="Lorie Van Auken">
       Lorie Van Auken
      </a>
      , one of the
      <a href="/wiki/Jersey_Girls" title="Jersey Girls">
       Jersey Girls
      </a>
      , estimates that only 30% of their questions were answered in the final 9/11 Commission Report, published July 22, 2004.
     </p>
     <p>
      The
      <a href="/wiki/9/11_Family_Steering_Committee" title="9/11 Family Steering Committee">
       9/11 Family Steering Committee
      </a>
      produced a website summarizing the questions they had raised to the Commission, indicating which they believe had been answered satisfactorily, which they believe had been addressed but not answered satisfactorily, and which they believe had been generally ignored in or omitted from the Report.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62">
       <a href="#cite_note-62">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        62
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In addition, the 339-page book,
      <i>
       The 9/11 Commission Report: Omissions and Distortions
      </i>
      , by
      <a href="/wiki/David_Ray_Griffin" title="David Ray Griffin">
       David Ray Griffin
      </a>
      , claimed the report had either omitted information or distorted the truth, providing 115 examples of his allegations.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63">
       <a href="#cite_note-63">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        63
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64">
       <a href="#cite_note-64">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        64
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65">
       <a href="#cite_note-65">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        65
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He has characterized the 9/11 Commission Report as "a 571-page lie".
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66">
       <a href="#cite_note-66">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        66
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      On May 26, 2008 adjunct religious studies professor Blair Gadsby began a protest and a hunger strike outside the offices of
      <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">
       Senator
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">
       Republican Party
      </a>
      nominee for President
      <a href="/wiki/John_McCain" title="John McCain">
       John McCain
      </a>
      's office requesting McCain meet with the principal scientists and leaders of the 9/11 Truth movement, specifically Richard Gage, Steven Jones, and David Ray Griffin. McCain had written the foreword to the book
      <i>
       Debunking 9/11 Myths: Why Conspiracy Theories Can't Stand Up to the Facts
      </i>
      , published by the magazine
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Popular_Mechanics" title="Popular Mechanics">
        Popular Mechanics
       </a>
      </i>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Benson_67-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Benson-67">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        67
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Arizona Republican State Senator Karen Johnson joined the protest in support. On June 10, Johnson with Gadsby as her guest and other 9/11 Truth movement members in the audience, spoke before the
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arizona_State_Senate" title="Arizona State Senate">
       Arizona State Senate
      </a>
      espousing the
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Controlled_demolition_hypothesis_for_the_collapse_of_the_World_Trade_Center" title="Controlled demolition hypothesis for the collapse of the World Trade Center">
       controlled demolition theory
      </a>
      and supporting a reopening of the 9/11 investigation.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-eastvalleytribune_16-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-eastvalleytribune-16">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        16
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Benson_67-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Benson-67">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        67
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      In response to a question, McCain said he did not meet Gadsby, adding:
      <i>
       "Because I don't take well to threats."
      </i>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68">
       <a href="#cite_note-68">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        68
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="NIST_Report_reaction">
       NIST Report reaction
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: NIST Report reaction">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:World_Trade_Center_9-11_Iron-rich_sphere.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1024" data-file-width="1024" height="240" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/World_Trade_Center_9-11_Iron-rich_sphere.jpg/240px-World_Trade_Center_9-11_Iron-rich_sphere.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/World_Trade_Center_9-11_Iron-rich_sphere.jpg/360px-World_Trade_Center_9-11_Iron-rich_sphere.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/World_Trade_Center_9-11_Iron-rich_sphere.jpg/480px-World_Trade_Center_9-11_Iron-rich_sphere.jpg 2x" width="240"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:World_Trade_Center_9-11_Iron-rich_sphere.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        An iron-rich sphere, found in the dust of the World Trade Center, as documented by the United States Geological Survey and RJ LeeGroup, Inc. RJ Lee's report states the spheres are indicative of molten iron.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">
         <a href="#cite_note-69">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          69
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">
         <a href="#cite_note-70">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          70
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
        Members of the 9/11 Truth movement claim the spheres indicate the presence of temperatures much hotter than office fires, or the presence of thermitic reactions.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71">
         <a href="#cite_note-71">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          71
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-active_thermitic_72-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-active_thermitic-72">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          72
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">
         <a href="#cite_note-73">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          73
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
        However, such spheres have been found to form when iron particles are affected by normal fuel fires.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">
         <a href="#cite_note-74">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          74
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Following the initial government investigation, the
      <a href="/wiki/Federal_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Federal Emergency Management Agency">
       Federal Emergency Management Agency
      </a>
      (FEMA) Report (May 2002)
      <a class="external text" href="http://wtc.nist.gov/reports_october05.htm" rel="nofollow">
       NIST Report
      </a>
      , numerous responses were written by members of the 9/11 Truth movement. Many of these responses claimed that it ignored key evidence suggesting an explosive demolition, "distorted reality" by using deceptive language and diagrams, and attacked
      <a href="/wiki/Straw_man" title="Straw man">
       straw man
      </a>
      arguments, such as the 2005 article by
      <a href="/wiki/Jim_Hoffman" title="Jim Hoffman">
       Jim Hoffman
      </a>
      entitled
      <i>
       Building a better mirage: NIST's 3-year $20,000,000 Cover Up of the Crime of the Century
      </i>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">
       <a href="#cite_note-75">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        75
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In late 2005,
      <a href="/wiki/Steven_E._Jones" title="Steven E. Jones">
       Steven E. Jones
      </a>
      , then a professor at
      <a href="/wiki/Brigham_Young_University" title="Brigham Young University">
       Brigham Young University
      </a>
      , announced a paper criticizing the NIST Report and describing his hypothesis that the WTC towers had been intentionally demolished by explosives. This paper garnered some mainstream media attention, including an appearance by Jones on
      <a href="/wiki/MSNBC" title="MSNBC">
       MSNBC
      </a>
      . This was the first such programming on a major cable news station. Jones was criticized by his university for making his claims public before vetting them through the approved peer review process. He was placed on paid leave and has since retired.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jones_53-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Jones-53">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        53
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DMorning_pleave_76-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-DMorning_pleave-76">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        76
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-USNW_BYUtakes_77-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-USNW_BYUtakes-77">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        77
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Accordingly, in April 2007, some 9/11 victims' family members and some members of the new
      <a class="external text" href="http://stj911.org/press_releases/NIST.html" rel="nofollow">
       Scholars for 9/11 Truth and Justice
      </a>
      submitted an additional request for correction to NIST, containing their own views on the defects in the report.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">
       <a href="#cite_note-78">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        78
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      NIST responded to this request in September 2007 supporting their original conclusions;
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79">
       <a href="#cite_note-79">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        79
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      the originators of the request wrote back to them in October 2007, asking them to reconsider their response.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Pamphlets_at_National_September_11_Museum">
       Pamphlets at National September 11 Museum
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Pamphlets at National September 11 Museum">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      Members of the movement distributed pamphlets that they say told the "truth" about the attacks at the
      <a href="/wiki/National_September_11_Memorial_%26_Museum" title="National September 11 Memorial &amp; Museum">
       National September 11 Memorial &amp; Museum
      </a>
      when the Museum opened in May 2014.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80">
       <a href="#cite_note-80">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        80
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81">
       <a href="#cite_note-81">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        81
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Organizations">
       Organizations
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Organizations">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Since the publication of the official reports, a number of interconnected 9/11 Truth movement organizations have been formed.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Architects_.26_Engineers_for_9.2F11_Truth">
       Architects &amp; Engineers for 9/11 Truth
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Architects &amp; Engineers for 9/11 Truth">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Architects_%26_Engineers_for_9-11_Truth_Banner.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="533" data-file-width="800" height="160" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Architects_%26_Engineers_for_9-11_Truth_Banner.jpg/240px-Architects_%26_Engineers_for_9-11_Truth_Banner.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Architects_%26_Engineers_for_9-11_Truth_Banner.jpg/360px-Architects_%26_Engineers_for_9-11_Truth_Banner.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Architects_%26_Engineers_for_9-11_Truth_Banner.jpg/480px-Architects_%26_Engineers_for_9-11_Truth_Banner.jpg 2x" width="240"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Architects_%26_Engineers_for_9-11_Truth_Banner.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Two people holding a banner of
        <i>
         Architects &amp; Engineers for 9/11 Truth
        </i>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="hatnote">
      See also:
      <a href="/wiki/Architects_%26_Engineers_for_9/11_Truth" title="Architects &amp; Engineers for 9/11 Truth">
       Architects &amp; Engineers for 9/11 Truth
      </a>
     </div>
     <p>
      Architects &amp; Engineers for 9/11 Truth is an organization of architectural and engineering professionals
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82">
       <a href="#cite_note-82">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        82
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      who support the
      <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Center_controlled_demolition_conspiracy_theories" title="World Trade Center controlled demolition conspiracy theories">
       World Trade Center controlled demolition conspiracy theories
      </a>
      and are calling for a new investigation into the destruction of the Twin Towers and WTC 7.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Olivier_12-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Olivier-12">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        12
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83">
       <a href="#cite_note-83">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        83
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The group is collecting signatures for a petition to the
      <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">
       United States Congress
      </a>
      that demands "a truly independent investigation with subpoena power" of the
      <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">
       September 11 attacks
      </a>
      , which, according to the organization, should include an inquiry into the possible use of explosives in the destruction of the World Trade Center buildings.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-telecinco_84-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-telecinco-84">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        84
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85">
       <a href="#cite_note-85">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        85
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Richard Gage, a
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Francisco_Bay_area" title="San Francisco Bay area">
       San Francisco Bay area
      </a>
      -based architect,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Moskowitz_86-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Moskowitz-86">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        86
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      founded
      <i>
       Architects &amp; Engineers for 9/11 Truth
      </i>
      in 2006.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rudin_4-4">
       <a href="#cite_note-Rudin-4">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        4
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87">
       <a href="#cite_note-87">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        87
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Investigations by the
      <a href="/wiki/Federal_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Federal Emergency Management Agency">
       Federal Emergency Management Agency
      </a>
      and the
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Institute_for_Standards_and_Technology" title="National Institute for Standards and Technology">
       National Institute for Standards and Technology
      </a>
      (NIST) have concluded that the buildings collapsed as a result of the impacts of the planes and of the fires that resulted from them.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYTCountersTheories_52-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-NYTCountersTheories-52">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        52
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88">
       <a href="#cite_note-88">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        88
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Gage criticized the government agency NIST for not having investigated the complete sequence of the
      <a href="/wiki/Collapse_of_the_World_Trade_Center" title="Collapse of the World Trade Center">
       collapse of the World Trade Center
      </a>
      towers
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Potocki_89-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Potocki-89">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        89
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and claims "the official explanation of the total destruction of the World Trade Center skyscrapers has explicitly failed to address the massive evidence for
      <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Center_controlled_demolition_conspiracy_theories" title="World Trade Center controlled demolition conspiracy theories">
       explosive demolition
      </a>
      ."
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">
       <a href="#cite_note-90">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        90
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      To support its position, the group Architects &amp; Engineers for 9/11 Truth points to the "free fall" pace of the collapse of the buildings, the "lateral ejection of steel", and to the "mid-air pulverization of concrete", among other things.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Beam-Slate_91-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Beam-Slate-91">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        91
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="9.2F11_Truth">
       9/11 Truth
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 9/11 Truth">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      <i>
       9/11 Truth
      </i>
      was launched in June 2004 and has become a central portal for many 9/11 Truth movement organizations. It is run by Janice Matthews (Executive Director),
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-washingtonpost_92-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-washingtonpost-92">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        92
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">
       <a href="#cite_note-93">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        93
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      David Kubiak (International Campaign Advisor)
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ID.3D855_94-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-ID.3D855-94">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        94
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and Mike Berger (Media Coordinator),
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNN_95-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-CNN-95">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        95
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      among others, and its advisory board includes Steven E. Jones and
      <a href="/wiki/Barrie_Zwicker" title="Barrie Zwicker">
       Barrie Zwicker
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_96-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-96">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        96
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      The organization co-sponsored opinion polls conducted by the U.S. market research and opinion polling firm
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zogby_International" title="Zogby International">
       Zogby International
      </a>
      that have shown substantial numbers of people believing the government did not tell the full truth about the September 11 attacks.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Scholars_for_9.2F11_Truth">
       Scholars for 9/11 Truth
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Scholars for 9/11 Truth">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      The original
      <i>
       Scholars for 9/11 Truth
      </i>
      was founded by
      <a href="/wiki/James_H._Fetzer" title="James H. Fetzer">
       James H. Fetzer
      </a>
      , a former philosophy professor, and physicist Steven E. Jones, in December 2005. It was a group of people of varying backgrounds and expertise who rejected the mainstream media and government account of the
      <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">
       September 11 attacks
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Barber_5-5">
       <a href="#cite_note-Barber-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">
       <a href="#cite_note-97">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        97
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Initially the group invited many ideas and hypotheses to be considered, however, leading members soon came to feel that the inclusion of some theories advocated by Fetzer  such as the use of directed energy weapons or miniature nuclear bombs to destroy the Twin Towerswere insufficiently supported by evidence and were exposing the group to ridicule. By December 2006, Jones and others set up a new scholars group,
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/9/11_truth_movement#Scholars_for_9.2F11_Truth_.26_Justice" title="9/11 truth movement">
       Scholars for 9/11 Truth and Justice
      </a>
      , whose focus is to use scientific analysis.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">
       <a href="#cite_note-98">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        98
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The original members took a vote on which group to join and the majority voted to move to the new group.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">
       <a href="#cite_note-99">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        99
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Scholars_for_9.2F11_Truth_.26_Justice">
       Scholars for 9/11 Truth &amp; Justice
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Scholars for 9/11 Truth &amp; Justice">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      Scholars for 9/11 Truth &amp; Justice (STJ) formed in January 2007 and is a self-described "group of scholars and supporters endeavoring to address the unanswered questions of the September 11, 2001 attack through scientific research and public education".
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">
       <a href="#cite_note-100">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        100
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The group is composed of more than 900 members,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">
       <a href="#cite_note-101">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        101
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      including
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Richard_Gage_(architect)" title="Richard Gage (architect)">
       Richard Gage
      </a>
      , Steven E. Jones,
      <a href="/wiki/Jim_Hoffman" title="Jim Hoffman">
       Jim Hoffman
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/David_Ray_Griffin" title="David Ray Griffin">
       David Ray Griffin
      </a>
      ,
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Peter_Phillips_(activist)" title="Peter Phillips (activist)">
       Peter Phillips
      </a>
      , and former Congressman
      <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Hamburg" title="Daniel Hamburg">
       Daniel Hamburg
      </a>
      . Most members support the conspiracy theory that the World Trade Center Towers and the third skyscraper, WTC 7, were destroyed through
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Controlled_demolition_hypothesis_for_the_collapse_of_the_World_Trade_Center" title="Controlled demolition hypothesis for the collapse of the World Trade Center">
       explosive demolition
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
         <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2014)">
          citation needed
         </span>
        </a>
       </i>
       ]
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In 2008 and 2009, several members of the Scholars for 9/11 Truth &amp; Justice published essays in science and engineering journals. In April 2008, a letter by some of its members, was published in
      <i>
       The Open Civil Engineering Journal
      </i>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">
       <a href="#cite_note-102">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        102
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      In July 2008, an article by Steven E. Jones and others was published in
      <i>
       The Environmentalist.
      </i>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">
       <a href="#cite_note-103">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        103
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In October 2008, a comment by STJ member James R. Gourley describing what he considers fundamental errors in a Baant and Verdure paper was included in an issue of the
      <i>
       Journal of Engineering Mechanics
      </i>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">
       <a href="#cite_note-104">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        104
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      In April 2009, Danish chemist and STJ member Niels H. Harrit, of the
      <a href="/wiki/University_of_Copenhagen" title="University of Copenhagen">
       University of Copenhagen
      </a>
      , and eight other authors, including some STJ members, published a paper in
      <i>
       The Open Chemical Physics Journal
      </i>
      , entitled
      <i>
       Active Thermitic Material Discovered in Dust from the 9/11 World Trade Center Catastrophe
      </i>
      . The paper, which caused the editor and only peer-reviewer, Professor Pileni, to resign, claiming it was published without her knowledge,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Videnskab_105-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Videnskab-105">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        105
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      concludes that chips consisting of unreacted and partially reacted
      <a href="/wiki/Nano-thermite" title="Nano-thermite">
       nano-thermite
      </a>
      ("super-thermite") appear to be present in samples of the dust.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-active_thermitic_72-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-active_thermitic-72">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        72
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Identifying_reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Identifying reliable sources">
         <span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (January 2013)">
          unreliable source?
         </span>
        </a>
       </i>
       ]
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">
       <a href="#cite_note-106">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        106
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="9.2F11_Citizens_Watch">
       9/11 Citizens Watch
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 9/11 Citizens Watch">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">
      Main article:
      <a href="/wiki/9/11_Citizens_Watch" title="9/11 Citizens Watch">
       9/11 Citizens Watch
      </a>
     </div>
     <p>
      9/11 Citizens Watch was formed in 2002 by John Judge and Kyle Hence and, along with the
      <a href="/wiki/9/11_Family_Steering_Committee" title="9/11 Family Steering Committee">
       Family Steering Committee
      </a>
      , played an active role in calling for the establishment of the 9/11 Commission, and monitoring the commission closely.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-csmonitor_107-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-csmonitor-107">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        107
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:William-rodriguez-american-scholars-symposium.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="409" data-file-width="477" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/3/37/William-rodriguez-american-scholars-symposium.jpg/170px-William-rodriguez-american-scholars-symposium.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/3/37/William-rodriguez-american-scholars-symposium.jpg/255px-William-rodriguez-american-scholars-symposium.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/3/37/William-rodriguez-american-scholars-symposium.jpg/340px-William-rodriguez-american-scholars-symposium.jpg 2x" width="170"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:William-rodriguez-american-scholars-symposium.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/William_Rodriguez" title="William Rodriguez">
         William Rodriguez
        </a>
        at American Scholars Symposium: 9/11 and the NeoCon Agenda in Los Angeles, California, June 2425, 2006
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="9.2F11_Commission_Campaign">
       9/11 Commission Campaign
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 9/11 Commission Campaign">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      Founded in 2011 by Senator
      <a href="/wiki/Mike_Gravel" title="Mike Gravel">
       Mike Gravel
      </a>
      , the 9/11 Commission Campaign's objective is to enact subpoena-capable, state-level commissions through state ballot initiatives, namely in Oregon, Alaska and California.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-911commissioncampaign_108-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-911commissioncampaign-108">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        108
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      These commissions are envisioned as citizen-driven, independent organizations that would form a semi-unified grassroots national presence by exercising
      <a href="/wiki/Joint_powers_authority" title="Joint powers authority">
       joint powers authority
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Hispanic_Victims_Group">
       Hispanic Victims Group
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=9/11_Truth_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Hispanic Victims Group">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      The Hispanic Victims Group is a group created after the 9/11 attacks, founded by
      <a href="/wiki/William_Rodriguez" title="William Rodriguez">
       William Rodriguez
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109">
       <a href="#cite_note-109">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        109
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      an adherent of the 9/11 Truth movement. The group was one of the key forces behind the creation of the 9/11 Commission.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-csmonitor_107-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-csmonitor-107">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        107
